 ) agar aap khaane ke shaukeen hai or pyaaj aapke swaad kaa ahm hissaa he to pyaaj kaatane ke dauraan aapane bhi kai baar aansu bahaae honge
 The more delicious the onion tastes, the more it makes you cry while cutting
 lekin aap chahen to kuch aasaan se upaay apanaakar bina roe pyaaj kaat sakate hai
 Why do tears come? During onion cutting, there is a chemical re-action and the gas comes out
 jab ye gas pani ke sampark main aati he to acid banataa he
 This is why our eyes start burning
 lekin aap chahen to pyaaj kaatane se pehle kuch chote-chote upaay karke is pareshaani se batch sakate hai
 1
 pyaaj ko thanda karke katempyaaj kaa chhilka utaar lijie
 After that, immerse it in water for some time and leave it
 aadhe ghante baad pyaaj kaaten
 Doing this will not irritate the eyes
 lekin pani main rakhane kii vajah se pyaaj chipchipa ho jayega
 In this case, carefully chop the onion
 2
 You can also use Vinegar
 If you want, you can peel onion and keep it in Vinegar and water solution for some time
 aisa karne se bhiankhon main aansu nahin aaenge
 3
 frij main rakhane ke baad katnapyaaj kaa chhilka utaar len or use kuch samay ke liye frij main rakh den
 Then cut the onion
 haalanki ye tarika bahut adhik prachlit nahin he kyonki aisa karne se frij membedboo aa jaati he
 4
 pyaaj ke upree hisse ko kaat dempyaaj kaatane kaa sabakaa apana tarikahota he
 But the best way to cut onion is by cutting the top portion of the onion first
 upree hisse ko kaat dene ke baad pyaaj kaatna kaaphi aasaan ho jayega
